---

### Post by sunexplodes on 2009-06-29
> **gymophett said:**
> What is your tint2 config? it's amazing!

Really, really small tweaks to the default one. removed the padding and the curvature from the tasks and made them darker. 

```
#---------------------------------------------
# TINT2 CONFIG FILE
#---------------------------------------------

#---------------------------------------------
# BACKGROUND AND BORDER
#---------------------------------------------
rounded = 0
border_width = 0
background_color = #000000 60
border_color = #ffffff 18

rounded = 0
border_width = 0
background_color = #666666 40
border_color = #ffffff 50

rounded = 0
border_width = 0
background_color = #333333 18
border_color = #ffffff 70

#---------------------------------------------
# PANEL
#---------------------------------------------
panel_monitor = all
panel_position = top center
panel_size = 100% 24
panel_margin = 0 0
panel_padding = 7 0
font_shadow = 0
panel_background_id = 1

#---------------------------------------------
# TASKBAR
#---------------------------------------------
taskbar_mode = single_monitor
taskbar_padding = 0 0 0
taskbar_background_id = 0

#---------------------------------------------
# TASKS
#---------------------------------------------
task_icon = 1
task_text = 1
task_width = 140
task_centered = 1
task_padding = 6 3
task_font = Calibri Bold 8
task_font_color = #ffffff 70
task_active_font_color = #ffffff 85
task_background_id = 3
task_active_background_id = 2

#---------------------------------------------
# SYSTRAYBAR
#---------------------------------------------
systray_padding = 0 4 5
systray_background_id = 0

#---------------------------------------------
# CLOCK
#---------------------------------------------
time1_format = %I:%M
time1_font = Calibri Bold 8
#time2_format = %A %d %B
#time2_font = sans 6
clock_font_color = #ffffff 76
clock_padding = 1 0
clock_background_id = 0

#---------------------------------------------
# BATTERY
#---------------------------------------------
battery = 0
battery_low_status = 7
battery_low_cmd = notify-send "battery low"
bat1_font = sans 8
bat2_font = sans 6
battery_font_color = #ffffff 76
battery_padding = 1 0
battery_background_id = 0


#---------------------------------------------
# MOUSE ACTION ON TASK
#---------------------------------------------
mouse_middle = none
mouse_right = close
mouse_scroll_up = toggle
mouse_scroll_down = iconify

```

---

They're part of a userstyle for Firefox.  I surgically removed the tab-specific code from an existing userstyle and then hacked it to pieces with a machete.  It's not quite finished yet. :)

### Post by andrek on 2009-06-30
Ok, use it with Stylish add-on

```
/*************************************
              TABS BAR
*************************************/

#browser .tabbrowser-tabs {
-moz-appearance: none !important;
visibility: visible !important; /* show tabs in full screen */
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tabs .tabs-container {
-moz-padding-start: 0px !important;
margin-left: -1px !important;
margin-right: -1px !important;
padding-bottom: 0px !important;
height: 25px !important;
border-bottom: solid 1px #848484 !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

/*.... fix to not show it in popups windows ....*/

#main-window[chromehidden="menubar toolbar directories extrachrome "] #browser .tabbrowser-tabs .tabs-container {
display: none !important;
}



/*************************************
                TABS
*************************************/

#browser .tabbrowser-tab {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
margin: 0px !important;
margin-right: -10px !important;
padding: 0px !important;
border: none !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] {
background: no-repeat url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAACMAAAAZCAIAAAA0WgDFAAAABnRSTlMAAAAAAABupgeRAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAkElEQVR42r3QSwqAMAyE4Vy8p3Lp1mP4Qhcqil7BgUCRkrYLk/wX+JihEELTdr19hHww4hwwigHzk0xn0Tdgg1mpNJqVSjjQY5PpgYI02SRIONBDYmw2SJYWg2QJB3pIjK3aZaVNu6yEA3fVKBewQ7WShFmnXlQI2KVXRcIsD4mxWymqBuzRqC7FGz0kxn72Ap8HO+o0tZbFAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC") !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[afterselected="true"] {
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}


/*.... FAVICON ....*/

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-icon-image {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
margin: 0px !important;
opacity: 0 !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] .tab-icon-image {
opacity: 1 !important;
}

/* add if tab icon is hidden */

#browser .tabbrowser-tab {
padding-left: 16px !important;
}

.tabbrowser-tab .tab-icon-image {
margin-left: 0px !important;
}

/*.... TEXT ....*/

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-text {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
padding-left: 4px !important;
padding-top: 6px !important;
height: 24px !important;
border: none !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] .tab-text {
background: url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAAZCAIAAAB/8tMoAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAQUlEQVR42l3FwQ0AIQgEwG3cTgENPMBIpAVzPO8xGRAR/pgZItJ/5pxtrQVVbWYGd0dEYO+Ncw4ys917UVVtjPEAy4xBX4HeLv8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=") !important;
font-weight: normal !important;
color: #000 !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] .tab-text {
opacity: 1 !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-text {
opacity: 0.3 !important;
}

/*.... CLOSE BUTTON ....*/

#browser .tab-close-button {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
display: block !important;
margin: 0px !important;
padding-right: 5px !important;
height: 20px !important;
width: 30px !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[beforeselected="true"] .tab-close-button {
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab:last-child .tab-close-button {
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] .tab-close-button,
#browser .tabbrowser-tab[last-tab="true"][selected="true"] .tab-close-button {
background: no-repeat url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAACMAAAAZCAIAAAA0WgDFAAAABnRSTlMAAAAAAABupgeRAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAiElEQVR42r3QuQ2AMABD0SyeqShpGYNLUAACwQq4AiXKgYSdt8CXbVq9qm6staZQBgpl1KU3Iy05g6CTcTLQy/gl0SD/Ol3Jz8CgUagUuA5GgUAGJoFCpfB1MLOFM7CwRUsrVfQ62KiiGdh5UoPg4ElliKXMIDhJMhm4GPKZ/6X8aQ/726eMMTenBjvqrYto1gAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==") !important;
}

/* icon */

#browser .tabbrowser-tab[selected="true"] .tab-close-button .toolbarbutton-icon {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
opacity: 1 !important;
}

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-close-button .toolbarbutton-icon {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
opacity: 0.3 !important;
}

#browser .tab-close-button,
#browser .tabs-closebutton,
#browser .findbar-closebutton {
-moz-image-region: rect(0, 16px, 16px, 0) !important;
list-style-image: url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABAAAAAwCAIAAACXPW0AAAAABnRSTlMAAAAAAABupgeRAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAABhElEQVR42mNgGH6gt3cHMnfKlL34VLe1bdHRSczMnAvhlpYuMzfPQzMCHSQlTbe2LiooWFxRsdLTs7GoaClhV5WVLff3bw8N7amvX0eUN4BmR0T0A60CupCw6uzs+R4eDTU1azo7t8XGTm5u3kggiExNc4AegHCBqn18WmbNOoRPz7Rp+5G5M2ceJMobo2DIAWA6ReaGhHTjUw1MORIS7sD8AOE6OlbKyweiGYEOgFlMUTHYzq7MxaVGQyPWwaGCsKucnKp0dJIMDNLc3OqI8gbQbCOjDKBVQBcSVm1jU6KhEQM029e31cQkG5itCQSRnJw/0AMQLlC1tnZCeHgfPj3AvI+HOwqGD5CW9kbmysj44lMtJeXJwaEuIuIA4YqJuXBx6aIZgQ6Ehe24ufVFRZ3ExV35+EzExJwJuwpoMD+/mYCAJTC7EuUNoNlA1UCrgC4krFpExJGX11hCwk1KyktIyEZS0oNAEHFx6QA9AOECVfPxmQKzFD49aOEoK+tHlDeoCQCkxWW1zJspAQAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==") !important;
}

#browser .tab-close-button:hover,
#browser .tabs-closebutton:hover,
#browser .findbar-closebutton:hover {
-moz-image-region: rect(16px, 16px, 32px, 0) !important;
}

#browser .tab-close-button:active,
#browser .tabs-closebutton:active,
#browser .findbar-closebutton:active {
-moz-image-region: rect(32px, 16px, 48px, 0) !important;
}

/*.... TABS BAR BUTTONS ....*/

#browser .tabs-container toolbarbutton {
-moz-appearance: none !important;
-moz-border-radius: 0px !important;
border: solid 1px #A0A0A0 !important;
border-top: none !important;
margin: 0px !important;
width: 18px !important;
opacity: 1 !important;
background: #ccc url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAAZCAIAAAB/8tMoAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAQUlEQVR42l3FwQ0AIQgEwG3cTgENPMBIpAVzPO8xGRAR/pgZItJ/5pxtrQVVbWYGd0dEYO+Ncw4ys917UVVtjPEAy4xBX4HeLv8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=") !important;
font-weight: normal !important;
color: #000 !important;
}

#browser .tabs-container toolbarbutton:hover {
background: url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAAZCAIAAAB/8tMoAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAQElEQVR42l3FwQ0AIQgEwO3ZMgGFBxiRYszxvMdkQET4Y2aISP+Zc7a1FlS1mRncHRGBvTfOOcjMdu9FVbUxxgPOVzxM1R3cYAAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==") !important;
}

#browser .tabs-container toolbarbutton:active {
background: url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAAZCAIAAAB/8tMoAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAPUlEQVR42l3FsQ0AMQgEsFuXEQMJFCAIW0VP+YVlrLXwx8wQkfmz9x7nHKjqMDO4+4gIZCaqatx70d2DiB7E7DcG+PycYwAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==") !important;
}

/*.... CLOSE BUTTON ....*/

#browser .tab-close-button {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
display: block !important;
margin: 0px !important;
padding-right: 5px !important;
height: 25px !important;
width: 35px !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

/* fix for many extensions compatibility */

#browser .tabs-container toolbarbutton {
margin-left: -1px !important;
}

/* scroll buttons icon */

/*.... NEW TAB BUTTON ....*/

#browser .tabs-container .tabbrowser-arrowscrollbox toolbarbutton.tabs-newtab-button {
margin-left: 10px !important;
margin-right: 8px !important;
width: 27px !important;
border: none !important;
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabs-container .tabbrowser-arrowscrollbox toolbarbutton.tabs-newtab-button:hover {
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

#browser .tabs-container .tabbrowser-arrowscrollbox toolbarbutton.tabs-newtab-button:active {
background: #BFBFBF !important;
}

.tabs-newtab-button:not(:hover) .toolbarbutton-icon {
display:none !important;
}


/*************************************
         LIST ALL TABS BUTTON
*************************************/

.tabs-alltabs-button {
display:none !important;
}
.tabbrowser-strip {
height: 25px
}
```

It will look like this :

[[img]http://f.imagehost.org/t/0669/firefox.jpg[/img]](http://f.imagehost.org/view/0669/firefox)

To get it fit well with your gtk theme, change #BFBFBF to anything you want.


I removed favicons from "non-selected" tabs, you can get them back by modyfing :
```

/*.... FAVICON ....*/

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-icon-image {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
margin: 0px !important;
opacity: **0** !important;
}
```
into
```

/*.... FAVICON ....*/

#browser .tabbrowser-tab .tab-icon-image {
-moz-appearance:none!important;
margin: 0px !important;
opacity: **0.3** !important;
}
```
